			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">SAN DIEGO </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x2014;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">January 9, 2023</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &#x2015; WD-40 Company (NASDAQ:WDFC),</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> today </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">reported financial results for its </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> fiscal quarter ended </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">November 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">22</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">.</font>

In EMEA</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we&#x2019;ve experienced </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">significant </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">headwinds from fluctuating currency exchange rates</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">a lower level of customer orders</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">weaker economic conditions,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a reduction in sales linked</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> our</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">decision to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">suspen</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">d</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales in Russia</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in 2022</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201D;</font>
		</p>

We shared with investors last quarter that we expected</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">much of our topline growth </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in fiscal year 2023 </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">would be weighted toward the second half of the fiscal year.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">W</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">e &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">expect </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">volume performance to improve in the second half of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">the fiscal year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> as price-related disruptions abate</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, and accordingly, today we are reiterating our guidance for the full fiscal year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201D; Brass concluded.</font>

In Canada</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales remained constant period over period. 		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Net sales of maintenance products, which are considered the primary growth focus for the Company, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">decreased 8 percent in the first quarter when compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. This decrease was primarily due to lower sales of WD-40</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Multi-Use Product</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which decreased 12 percent compared to the prior fiscal year quarter. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">This decline was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> driven by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">lower </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales volume</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> linked to recent pricing actions which resulted in a lower level of customer orders and promotional programs.&nbsp;&nbsp;Sales declines </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> also due to unfavorable changes in foreign currency exchanges rates and weaker economic conditions in some regions. </font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Dividend and Share Repurchase Update</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As previously announced, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared on Tuesday, December 13, 2022</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">a quarterly dividend of $0.83 per share reflecting an increase of more than 6 percent compared to the previous quarter&#x2019;s dividend.&nbsp;&nbsp;The quarterly dividend is payable on January 31, 2023 to stockholders of record at the close of business on January 13, 2023.</font>
		</p>

Under the plan</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> the Company is authorized to acquire up to $75.0 million of its outstanding shares through August 31, 2023. The timing and amount of repurchases will be based on terms and conditions acceptable to the Company and in c</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">ompliance with applicable laws and regulations. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">During the period from November 1, 2021 through November 30, 2022, the Company repurchased&nbsp;160,982 shares at a total cost of&nbsp;$33.2&nbsp;million under this $75.0 million plan.</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">During the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">first quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, the Company repurchased 22,420 shares at a total cost of&#x202F;$4.1&#x202F;million under this $75.0 million plan.</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

Such statements reflect the Company&#x2019;s current expectations with respect to currently available operating, financial and economic information.&nbsp;&nbsp;These forward-looking statements are subject to certain risks, uncertainties and assumptions that could cause actual results to differ materially from those anticipated in or implied by the forward-looking statements. These forward-looking statements are generally identified with words such as &#x201C;believe,&#x201D; &#x201C;expect,&#x201D; &#x201C;intend,&#x201D; &#x201C;plan,&#x201D; &#x201C;could,&#x201D; &#x201C;may,&#x201D; &#x201C;aim,&#x201D; &#x201C;anticipate,&#x201D; &#x201C;target,&#x201D; &#x201C;estimate&#x201D; and similar expressions.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>
